[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability was detected in the Wireshark JSON dissector [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring fuzzing with AddressSanitizer. The issue occurs when processing JSON strings[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontaining Unicode surrogate pairs, specifically during the `json_string_unescape` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction execution. The vulnerability involves a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte read operation beyond the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds of a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte allocated heap buffer.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Details[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a **heap-buffer-overflow** vulnerability with a severity score of [0m[1;36m12[0m[39m [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte-read-heap-buffer-overflow[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The error occurs at address `[0m[1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[39m`, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is located exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after a [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte allocated region `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0x50300012dcc0[0m[39m,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x50300012dcd3[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. This indicates an off-by-one error where the code attempts to [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mread one byte past the end of the allocated buffer.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Call Stack Analysis[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests through the following execution path:[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Entry Point**: The fuzzer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_json`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m processes a test case containing [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJSON data with Unicode surrogate pairs[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **JSON Processing Chain**:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_json` initiates JSON parsing[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `tvbparse_get` and `execute_callbacks` handle the parsing logic[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `after_value` processes parsed values[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `get_json_string` extracts JSON string values[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **`json_string_unescape` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;92m361:29[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: The actual overflow occurs here [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring string unescaping[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Memory Allocation Context[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe problematic buffer was allocated through the following sequence:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `realloc` in `g_realloc`[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `wmem_strbuf_finalize` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;92m388:25[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/wsutil/wmem/[0m[95mwmem_strbuf.c[0m[39m`[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Called from `get_json_string` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mLine [0m[1;92m564:11[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis suggests the buffer size calculation or finalization process may not properly [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maccount for the full length of the unescaped string.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Triggering Input[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer generated a test case containing:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m[39m\n  [0m[32m"surrogates"[0m[39m: [0m[32m"\\U0000d83d\\U0000"[0m[39m\n[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m\n\n[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis input contains:[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- JSON object with a [0m[32m"surrogates"[0m[39m key[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Unicode escape sequences: `\U0000d83d` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpartial surrogate pair[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `\U0000` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mincomplete sequence[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The malformed or incomplete Unicode sequences appear to trigger the buffer [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow during unescaping[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Key Observations[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Location**: The overflow occurs in [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m, column [0m[1;36m29[0m[39m within the [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`json_string_unescape` function[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Buffer Size**: The allocated buffer is only [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m bytes, which appears [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient for the unescaped string data[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Unicode Handling**: The vulnerability is triggered by specific Unicode escape [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences, particularly surrogate pairs[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Off-by-One Pattern**: Reading exactly [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes beyond the buffer boundary [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msuggests a classic off-by-one error in bounds checking or length calculation[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis Summary[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter thoroughly analyzing the code snippets and evaluation report, I have [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified the root cause of the heap-buffer-overflow vulnerability:[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Root Cause**: The `json_string_unescape` function in [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m` has a single vulnerable loop at [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m that reads [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m hex digits for a `\U` trail surrogate without performing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary checks or hex digit validation. This is the ONLY loop in the entire [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction missing these critical safety checks.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Triggering Condition**: The input `\U0000d83d\U0000` contains:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. A valid lead surrogate: `\U0000d83d` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0xd83d[0m[39m is a lead surrogate[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. An incomplete trail surrogate: `\U0000` [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m hex digits instead of required [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mWhen processing the incomplete trail surrogate, the buggy loop attempts to read [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhex digits but only [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m are available, causing it to read past the input buffer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mboundary.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Critical Observations**:[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. All other similar loops in the function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m341[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m422[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m472[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m properly implement boundary checks and validation[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. The vulnerable loop follows the exact same pattern as these correct loops but is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmissing the safety checks[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. The code already has proper error handling infrastructure via the [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`is_valid_unicode_character` flag[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. This appears to be an accidental omission during development/refactoring[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Patch Location[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File**: `[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-json.c[0m[39m`  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Function**: `json_string_unescape`  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Lines**: [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthe vulnerable loop[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Implementation[0m                                                            [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the loop at lines [0m[1;36m359[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m368[0m[39m to add two critical safety checks that are present[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min all other similar loops:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Boundary Check** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfollowing pattern from line [0m[1;36m272[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Before reading `string[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mread_index[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`, verify that `read_index < string_length`[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If boundary exceeded, set `is_valid_unicode_character = false` and break[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Hex Digit Validation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfollowing pattern from line [0m[1;36m283[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This Is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: Only adds safety checks to the one vulnerable location, [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39min [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m other similar loops throughout the same function [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m272[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m276[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m283[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m287[0m[39m, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m322[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m326[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m333[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m337[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m425[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m429[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m436[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m440[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m475[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m479[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m486[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m490[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **No Behavioral Change for Valid Input**: For correctly formatted Unicode escape[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequences, the checks pass transparently - no impact on normal operation[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Graceful Error Handling**: For malformed input, uses the existing error [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandling framework:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Sets `is_valid_unicode_character = false`[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Breaks from loop safely[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Falls through to existing error handling at lines [0m[1;36m410[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[39m which appends [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mUnicode replacement character [0m[1;39m([0m[39mU+FFFD[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Root Cause Fix**: Directly addresses the identified vulnerability without [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifying any unrelated code[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Error Handling Flow**: The `is_valid_unicode_character` flag is already used [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthroughout the function for error tracking. The fix integrates seamlessly with this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting mechanism.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Surrogate Pair Processing**: The logic for combining lead and trail surrogates[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m370[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m377[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged. Valid surrogate pairs will continue to be [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessed correctly.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m Output**: The final UTF-[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m conversion and output [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m396[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m413[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munchanged. The fix only affects input validation during the reading phase.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **No Impact on Other Escape Sequences**: All other escape sequence handlers [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`\u`, `\n`, `\t`, etc.[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are unmodified and continue to work as before.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Evaluation Report Issues[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Heap-Buffer-Overflow**: The boundary check `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;39m([0m[39mread_index < [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstring_length[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` prevents reading beyond the input buffer, directly resolving the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreported heap-buffer-overflow at line [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Off-by-One Error**: The check prevents the exact scenario described in the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreport where code attempts to read [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the [0m[1;36m19[0m[39m-byte buffer.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Unicode Surrogate Pair Handling**: Properly validates incomplete `\U` trail [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msurrogate sequences like `\U0000` in the test input `\U0000d83d\U0000`.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Malformed Input Handling**: Converts crashes on malformed input into graceful [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdegradation with replacement character output.[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: Malformed Unicode escape sequences that previously crashed will [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnow be replaced with the Unicode replacement character [0m[1;39m([0m[39mU+FFFD[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is actually the INTENDED behavior as evidenced by:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Existing error handling throughout the function that uses the same replacement [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcharacter approach[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Similar handling in other loops for invalid sequences[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Wireshark's philosophy of robust parsing that doesn't crash on malformed input[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Testing Considerations**: The fix should be validated with:[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The original fuzzer test case that triggered the bug[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Valid surrogate pairs [0m[1;39m([0m[39mboth `\u` and `\U` variants[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Incomplete escape sequences of various lengths[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Invalid hex characters in escape sequences[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other JSON escape sequences to ensure no regression[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in the Codebase[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the exact pattern already implemented [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m times in the same function:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Lines [0m[1;36m269[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m291[0m[39m: `\U` initial code point parsing[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Lines [0m[1;36m319[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m341[0m[39m: `\U` lead + `\u` trail surrogate[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Lines [0m[1;36m422[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m444[0m[39m: `\u` initial code point parsing  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Lines [0m[1;36m472[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m494[0m[39m: `\u` lead + `\u` trail surrogate[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis demonstrates that the solution is proven, tested, and part of the original [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesign intent. The vulnerable loop was simply missing these checks due to an [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moversight.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
